It also supports vector shapes such as rectangle, ellipse, line, and both static and dynamic text/barcode fields. Users will be able to retrieve address and contact information from the Microsoft People’s app with just a few taps and have the information printed out in a snap.\r\n \r\nThe app comes with capabilities such as Grid Snapping, Zooming, Rulers, Label Stock Customization, Undo/Redo, Objects Alignment, Multi-Objects Selection and WYSIWYG user interfaces – features found only in industrial strength desktop labeling software. Both the Inch and Centimeter measurement units are supported.\r\n\r\nThe app is capable of creating Code 39, Industrial 2 of 5 and POSTNET barcode using TrueType fonts. This is important for printing high quality barcode labels as it allows high resolution printing and produces barcodes that are sharp and accurate. The high resolution barcodes also ensures requirements of industry specifications such as those by GS1 and ISO can be met with ease. The QR Code 2D barcode is also supported and is generated using a high resolution image.\r\n\r\nThe app is designed to work on both tablet and desktop mode on Windows  and supports users using either the touch or mouse input interface.\r\n \r\nOur Philosophy\r\n\r\nHave you ever thought about how many times you need to use or reuse your barcode and labels? Every day, day after day, label after label and barcode after barcode. We definitely have. That is why we make our barcode and label app to be simple, elegant and easy to use. \r\n\r\nWe have tested our app vigorously, so that you can be assured of its quality, robustness and reliability. Our app is designed in black and white color. We believe this is how a professional barcode and label app should be implemented. \r\n\r\nWhether you are a business owner, manager, manufacturer, or business executive from a Fortune 500 company, or a consultant or an entrepreneur joining the business world, we hope that you will find this barcode and label app useful as we have drawn deeply from our past experience, put in our best effort and invested much time to develop it.\r\n\r\nTips\r\n1. You can create an object by selecting a Shape on the Toolbar and then dragging your finger or mouse on the label. \r\n2. You can double tap or click on an object to bring up the Properties dialog.\r\n\r\nUpdate Logs\r\nv3.91\r\nFixed the crash if contacts permission is not granted to the app\r\n\r\nv3.9\r\nSupport for
